Pro Tour–San Diego Standard Deck Lists: A-F
===========================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 21, 2010 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast











This page includes deck lists from players who recorded up to 17 points in the 10 Standard rounds. To see lists of players recording 18 or more points, [click here](http://archive.wizards.com/magic/magazine/article.aspx?x=mtg/daily/eventcoverage/ptsd10/topstddecks).







#### Hector Alonso Perez Del Valle
